shared_focus = {
	id = YAL_subsidize_industry
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_industry_2
	x = 6
	y = 0
	cost = 7.00
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 80
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus YAL_subsidize_industry"
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = industrial_bonus
			bonus = 1.0
			uses = 2
			category = industry
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
}

			}
		}
	}

}

shared_focus = {
	id = YAL_establish_ordenstaat_flussland
	icon = GFX_goal_river_fed_suppression
	x = -1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = YAL_second_grand_crusade
	cost = 7.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = YAL_second_grand_crusade
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = YAL_establish_freistaat_flussland
	}
	available = {
		DMT = {
			exists = no
		}
		BAK = {
			exists = no
		}
		DEP = {
			exists = no
		}

		}

		}

			exists = no
		}
		NIM = {
			exists = no
		}
		FRE = {
			exists = no
		}
		ZES = {
			exists = no
		}
		OLV = {
			exists = no
		}
		FIR = {
			exists = no
		}
		FBK = {
			exists = no
		}
		WAT = {
			exists = no
		}
		NCH = {
			exists = no
		}
		BAR = {
			exists = no
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 40
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus YAL_establish_ordenstaat_flussland"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					RIV = { exists = yes }
				}
				RIV = {
					clr_country_flag = river_federation_founder
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					clear_variable = annexed_riv_members
				}
				clear_global_event_target = RivFed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HLQ = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = HLQ }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LNS = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = LNS }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				LSM = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = LSM }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				LSC = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = LSC }
		}
		release_puppet = RCT
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				has_character = LSM_konrada_wavewing
			}
			LSM_konrada_wavewing = {
				set_nationality = RCT
			}
		}
		RCT = {
			RIV_leave_fed_no_ally = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = RCT_ordenstaat
			hidden_effect = {
				#load_focus_tree = rivercity_ordenstaat
				load_focus_tree = generic_griffon_focus
				retire_country_leader = yes
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = YAL_RCT_fasc_party_long
				name = YAL_RCT_fasc_party
			}
			add_popularity = { 
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.5
			}
			LSM_konrada_wavewing = {
				promote_character = holy_order_n
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = NIM
					is_core_of = BAK
					is_core_of = FRE
					is_core_of = DMT
					is_core_of = DEP
					is_core_of = WIT
					is_core_of = LCT
					is_core_of = ZES
					is_core_of = OLV
					is_core_of = FIR
					is_core_of = FBK
					is_core_of = WAT
					is_core_of = NCH
					is_core_of = BAR
				}
				# Some Riverland Nations might get cores on states of these tags, but the Empire should not cede states that it can integrate, therefore exclude
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						is_core_of = LUS
						is_core_of = GRY
						is_core_of = HQL
						is_core_of = LNS
						is_core_of = LSM
						is_core_of = LSC
						is_core_of = GRU
						is_core_of = BRF
						is_core_of = GRW
					}
				}
			}
			add_core_of = RCT
			RCT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

				}
			}
		}

				}
			}
		}

	}

		if = {

				JER = {
					exists = yes
					has_government = communism
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			country_event = yale.145
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HEL = {
					exists = yes
					has_government = communism
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			country_event = yale.145

				name = special_forces_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 2
				category = para_tech
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
}
